# Корпус данеток — справочный материал

Используйте примеры для анализа структуры и механизмов. Не копируйте персонажей, предметы и причинные цепочки.

## dnk_0f469fee29743ebd — The Death Row Inmate and the Demon

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.96  
Теги: Supernatural_Fantasy, real-user-guesses  

**Условие:** A death row inmate met a demon and made a wish. The demon helped him. A few days later, pedestrians on the street were holding their noses and looking disgusted.

**Разгадка:** The demon turned the inmate invisible, allowing him to successfully escape prison. However, he was hit and killed by a car on the road. A few days later, his body began to rot and stink, which was unbearable for the passersby.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The inmate's wish was about not being seen.
- He successfully escaped from prison.
- The wish granted by the demon led to his death.
- He died in a traffic accident.
- His body was left on the road.
- The body was only noticed days later due to the smell of decay.
- His invisibility was the cause of the accident.

## dnk_11b52ff114f947f3 — The Woman in the Pink Dress

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.96  
Теги: Clever_Logic, real-user-guesses  

**Условие:** Your new neighbor is a young man who lives alone. One day, coming home after a late-night snack, you see a long-haired woman in a pink dress and heavy makeup enter your neighbor's apartment. Late at night, you hear arguing and things being thrown from next door, which is especially loud in the quiet hallway. The next day, in the trash bag outside your neighbor's door, you see a shredded pink dress and a lock of long hair. You ask your neighbor about it, but he stammers and won't say anything... Should you call the police? What happened?

**Разгадка:** The neighbor is a man with a cross-dressing fetish, which is why he has always been single. His family doesn't know about this and has been pressuring him to get married, so he moved out of his parents' house. That day, the neighbor was coming home after being dressed as a woman, and you saw him. Unexpectedly, his mother was already waiting for him at home. Seeing her son in women's clothing, they had a huge fight, and the mother cut up his pink dress and wig. This is what you saw.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The 'woman' in the pink dress was the neighbor himself.
- The neighbor is a man who cross-dresses.
- The late-night argument was between the neighbor and his mother.
- The neighbor's mother discovered his cross-dressing.
- The mother was very angry about it.
- The mother shredded the neighbor's pink dress.
- The mother cut up the neighbor's wig.
- The neighbor stammered because he wanted to hide his cross-dressing.
- The neighbor's family does not accept his hobby.
- The items in the trash bag were the result of a family conflict, not evidence of a crime.

## dnk_46e8bbd59d4cdffe — The Ritual

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.96  
Теги: Clever_Logic, real-user-guesses  

**Условие:** Lately, your parents have been arguing a lot. You also feel your mother has been acting strangely. She's always distracted, secretly asking you how to transfer money to others... Sometimes she waves her hands silently at home as if performing some ritual. One evening after dinner, your father went out for a walk, and your mother also quietly left. Already suspicious, you followed her... Ah, so that's what it was...

**Разгадка:** Your mother was practicing for her public square dancing group. Your father thought she was having an affair. The money transfer was to buy team outfits for dancing, and the hand-waving was to practice the dance moves. To avoid disturbing the neighbors, all the square-dancing ladies wear headphones and dance in silence, which looks like they're performing some mysterious ritual.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The mother's strange behavior was square dancing.
- The father misunderstood the mother's actions.
- The father suspected the mother was having an affair.
- The mother asked about transferring money to buy dance costumes.
- The mother waving her hands was her practicing dance moves.
- The 'silence' was because they were dancing with headphones on.
- Dancing with headphones was to avoid disturbing the neighbors.
- The mother sneaking out was to go dance with her group.
- The parents' arguments stemmed from the father's misunderstanding.

## dnk_568e2da11fb9ba02 — Counting

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.96  
Теги: Crime_Thriller, real-user-guesses  

**Условие:** I was counting, and he was counting too. I was terrified.

**Разгадка:** I live in a high-rise building. Today, out of boredom, I looked out the window and accidentally witnessed a crime in the opposite building. A man seemed to have stabbed someone to death. I quickly took out my phone to call the police. The police asked for the floor where the incident occurred, so I started counting the floors to the man's level. When I reached his floor, I realized the man had noticed me and was counting the floors up to my level, holding a bloody knife and smiling eerily!

**Ключевые факты:**

- I and the person in the opposite building were looking at each other through the windows.
- The counting was to determine the floor number.
- I was counting to specify a location.
- A terrible event happened at that location.
- The other person was counting the floors towards me.
- The other person wanted to kill me.
- I am in danger.

## dnk_6297d8959b47e0f2 — The News

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.96  
Теги: Crime_Thriller, real-user-guesses  

**Условие:** A man came home from work, turned on the TV to watch the news, and then fainted from shock.

**Разгадка:** The man worked at a haunted house and was responsible for cleaning up after it closed. The haunted house had many prop corpses. While cleaning, he saw a very realistic prop corpse. He didn't think much of it, marveling at the craftsmanship as he cleaned. After work, he went home, turned on the TV, and saw a news report about a missing person case. The report showed a photo of the missing person, who was the same person as the realistic prop he had seen in the haunted house. He fainted from shock.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The man's workplace is a haunted house.
- The man's job involves handling horror props.
- He saw a very realistic 'corpse' at work.
- He initially thought the realistic corpse was a prop.
- The man watched the TV news after getting home from work.
- The news reported a missing person case.
- The news showed a photo of the missing person.
- The missing person's photo matched the 'corpse' he saw at the haunted house.
- The man realized what he saw was not a prop, but a real body.
- He fainted from the shock.

## dnk_9e6e199ff9cf318e — The Slide

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.96  
Теги: Supernatural_Fantasy, real-user-guesses  

**Условие:** Near programmer Wang's home, there is a park. Every day when Wang passed the park on his way home from working overtime, he would see a child in a plaid shirt standing by the slide with a terrified look. One day, Wang didn't work overtime and, on a whim, went down the slide. After sliding down, Wang was horrified. What did he see?

**Разгадка:** It turned out Wang saw himself on his way home from work. The slide was a time machine. When Wang slid down, he turned into the child. The child's plaid shirt was actually programmer Wang's. The terrified child he saw every time was himself after sliding down.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The slide has an unnatural function.
- The slide is related to time.
- The terrified child seen every day is the same person.
- The child's plaid shirt is related to Wang.
- After sliding down, Wang saw himself.
- Sliding down caused a change in age.
- The child was the younger version of Wang himself.

## dnk_c6647a60c242b8d9 — The Lost Phone

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.96  
Теги: Crime_Thriller, real-user-guesses  

**Условие:** My phone was missing. When I found it, I was terrified.

**Разгадка:** I went clubbing with my best friend. After drinking a bit and dancing, I sat down to rest and realized my phone was gone. I asked my friend to call my number. A strange man's voice answered, but the club was too loud, and he hung up before we could ask anything. I went home feeling dejected, only to find my phone on my bedside table. I suddenly remembered I hadn't taken my phone out with me at all today, and I've always lived alone. I couldn't help but feel a chill down my spine...

**Ключевые факты:**

- 'I' thought the phone was lost outside.
- Someone answered the call 'I' made to the lost phone.
- The person who answered was a strange man.
- The phone was eventually found in 'my' house.
- 'I' live alone.
- 'I' did not take the phone out that day.
- A stranger had entered the house.

## dnk_007f6d8ba3a4418e — The Girl Who Jumped

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.95  
Теги: Supernatural_Fantasy  

**Условие:** A college girl was working part-time during her vacation and not living at home. One night, she heard a noise and the sound of a door opening downstairs, so she immediately hid under the bed. The next day, she was found dead under the bed. Please deduce.

**Разгадка:** A girl had previously jumped to her death from the dormitory building. That day happened to be the seventh day after her death, and she returned to find a replacement. Since the girl died by jumping, her ghost maintained an upside-down posture. When she entered the room, she came face-to-face with the girl hiding under the bed, who died of fright.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The girl died of extreme fright.
- Someone had recently committed suicide by jumping from the dormitory building.
- The event occurred on the 'seventh day' after the death, a significant day in some traditions.
- The noise was made by the ghost of the girl who jumped.
- The ghost maintained the posture it had at the time of death.
- The ghost's posture was head-down, feet-up.
- The girl hiding under the bed saw the ghost's face.
- The ghost entered the room upside down.

## dnk_00cdb276ecbc3e84 — Pregnant

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.95  
Теги: Mind_Game  

**Условие:** I'm pregnant... but ever since my sister came to my house, I'm the only one left in the house.

**Разгадка:** My husband and I were very much in love. Shortly after we got married, I became pregnant. We finally had our first child, but I developed postpartum depression because of it. My mental state got worse and worse, and I had a strong lack of security. I imagined my child as my 'sister'. I saw that whenever the 'sister' cried, my husband would rush to comfort her, and even when the 'sister' ate, my husband had to feed her. I felt very angry and jealous. Why should my husband care so much for this 'sister'? He said he would only love me in his life. Overwhelmed by anger and jealousy, I killed both of them in a fit of rage.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The narrator recently gave birth to a child.
- The narrator's mental state became unstable after childbirth.
- The 'sister' mentioned in the story actually refers to the baby.
- The narrator misunderstood and became jealous of her husband's care for the baby.
- The other people in the house were killed by the narrator.

## dnk_0170c6bab4547539 — Bloody Prosperity

Качество: 0.95  
Теги: Crime_Thriller  

**Условие:** That winter when many starved in cities, a mountain town's lumber industry strangely flourished. Why?

**Разгадка:** During famine, urbanites returned to rural areas seeking food. Townspeople killed returnees, using their bodies as fertilizer to enrich poor soil for premium lumber - bringing prosperity built on mass murder.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The prosperity came from deaths
- Returnees were all murdered
- Bodies became tree fertilizer
- Premium lumber came from human remains
- Prosperity masked horrific crimes

## dnk_01a21ad2948a4351 — Auction

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.95  
Теги: Clever_Logic  

**Условие:** Sam is a kind-hearted rich man. One day, he bid high at an auction for something he didn’t like. Six months later, he noticed that everyone except him at the auction had died. He felt proud of his actions.

**Разгадка:** He was invited to an auction disguised as a charity event, but it was actually an auction for 'female slaves' organized by a criminal group. These slaves were female assassins, whose mission was to enter wealthy homes, rob them, and kill the owners. To protect these women from further exploitation, Sam bid high on one of the slaves and took her home. Sam treated her like a daughter, and the assassin was moved and quietly left his house. The other wealthy men were not so fortunate and were killed, their wealth stolen.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The auction was not charity-based
- The item bought was a human being
- The item was inherently dangerous
- The rich man’s kindness saved his own life
- The other wealthy men were killed

## dnk_01ec3267ba8942ec — Destruction

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.95  
Теги: Original_Data  

**Условие:** This time, my work will destroy everyone.

**Разгадка:** Back then, when I was just starting out, I didn't understand the unwritten rules and refused the critics' hints for bribes. As a result, my debut work received overwhelmingly negative reviews, and I myself was labeled notorious. Later, I learned the ways of the world, built good relationships with them through various means, and my works began to receive rave reviews. Today, I have become what people call an 'artist,' but I have never forgotten the initial humiliation. This time, I have meticulously prepared a shockingly bad film; every shot is infused with my fire of revenge. I can't wait to see how, when those critics who took my money praise this 'masterpiece' against their conscience, the discerning eyes of the audience will nail them to the pillar of shame. That day will be the day of their ruin and disgrace, and also the time for my sweet revenge.

**Ключевые факты:**

- My profession is a director or artist.
- 'Destruction' is not physical but refers to the destruction of reputation.
- The 'everyone' to be destroyed specifically refers to those corrupt critics.
- This 'work' is a terrible film I deliberately produced.
- The critics, having received benefits from me, have to praise it against their conscience.
- My ultimate goal is revenge, to make these critics lose their reputation and be disgraced.

- The means used for 'salvation' is a common liquid, usually considered blue.
- The fatal factor represented by the color 'black' is produced by the 'red' process of destruction.
- The event took place in a building.
- Despite the 'blue' rescue efforts, 'black' still caused fatalities.

**Разгадка:** The four men were carrying a coffin. The fifth person was lying in the coffin, already dead.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The fifth person was lying in the coffin
- He didn’t need to hurry because he was already dead
- The four men were soaked while carrying the coffin
- The coffin protected the fifth person from getting wet

## dnk_03ff9ace6e5d521f — Hide-and-Seek

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.95  
Теги: Constant_Change  

**Условие:** Mom taught me to play hide-and-seek, the rules were different from when I played with friends. I won, Mom died.

**Разгадка:** I am 7 years old. My dad, mom, and I were once a happy family of three. But ever since Dad started drinking heavily, everything changed. He turned into a monster I didn't recognize. He started hitting Mom for no reason, each time beating her until she wouldn't move before he would stop. Once, after hitting Mom, he saw me crying loudly nearby. He raised his fist and walked towards me. Mom, seeing this, desperately crawled up and rushed over to hold his leg. Dad beat Mom again until she couldn't move, then went into the house. The next day, while Dad was away, I asked Mom: 'Mom, how can we stop Dad from hitting us? I don't want to see you get hit anymore, it hurts me so much...' Mom, with tears in her eyes, smiled and said: 'Sweetie, let's play hide-and-seek, okay? If you win, we won't be hit anymore. But this game is different from when you play with your friends. In this game, Dad and I are both looking for you. If I find you, you win. If Dad finds you, then you run downstairs quickly, don't let Dad catch you, okay?' 'Okay, Mom, I understand!' Another night, Dad came back drunk again. Unsurprisingly, he beat Mom again with fists and kicks. After a while, seeing Mom motionless, Dad went back to his room to rest. After Mom saw him go back, she carefully crawled over to me, curled up in a ball, and said: 'Sweetie, let's start playing hide-and-seek now.' I immediately got up and hid in the large wardrobe in my bedroom, not daring to make a sound. Through the crack in the door, I vaguely saw Mom holding a fruit knife, walking into Dad's bedroom. After a sound of fighting and things breaking, Mom staggered out slowly. Mom opened the wardrobe where I was hiding and said: 'Sweetie won, Dad will never hit us again, Mom will always love you...' After saying that, Mom collapsed, and bright red blood kept flowing from her neck. Mom closed her eyes forever... It turned out that when Mom was trying to kill Dad, Dad wasn't fast asleep. He was awakened by Mom's footsteps, saw Mom holding the knife, and started to struggle for it. During the struggle, Mom's hand holding the knife was grabbed by Dad, and it cut Mom's carotid artery. Blood gushed out continuously. At this moment, Dad was stunned, and Mom took this opportunity to stab the fruit knife into Dad's heart.

**Ключевые факты:**

- This game of hide-and-seek was a plan designed by the mother to solve the problem of domestic violence.
- The peculiarity of the game rules (e.g., Mom finding the child means winning) was to protect the child and execute the plan.
- While the child was hiding, the mother took fatal action against the father.
- The father also died during this 'game'.
- The mother's cause of death was a fatal injury sustained during the struggle with the father.

## dnk_04ab61feb2ade4e8 — He

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.95  
Теги: Clever_Logic  

**Условие:** Great, he's dead
Oh no, he's not dead
Damn it, he's dead

**Разгадка:** He and I were generals of two opposing countries, deadlocked on the battlefield for many days. One day, I heard he was dead and happily ordered my troops to advance. Unexpectedly, I saw him again on the battlefield. I thought I had fallen into a trap and ordered a retreat. Later, I found out it was just his statue. I fell for his posthumous trick and missed the best opportunity to deploy my troops.

**Ключевые факты:**

- A visual misdirection was the key reason for the misjudgment (thinking the opponent wasn't dead).
- The opponent used a posthumous stratagem.
- The event takes place in the context of military confrontation or intense competition.
- The narrator's final regret is related to missing a strategic opportunity, not just the opponent's life or death.
- A non-living object was used as a key deception tool, creating the illusion that the opponent was still alive.

## dnk_0528de45f36a4db2 — Unexpectedly Young

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.95  
Теги: Clever_Logic  

**Условие:** One day, the idle Xiao Li was wandering the streets. He happened to be near a primary school as it was letting out. In the crowded stream of people, Xiao Li was unfortunately knocked over by a mischievous student, Xiao Ming. Not only did Xiao Ming not apologize, but he also provoked Xiao Li. However, Xiao Li wasn't angry and was instead very happy. Why?

**Разгадка:** Xiao Ming angrily said, 'Which class are you in?' Xiao Li, who was nearly 30, never expected to look so young in a primary schooler's eyes and felt much better about himself.

**Ключевые факты:**

- Xiao Li's actual age is close to 30.
- Xiao Ming is a primary school student.
- Xiao Ming said something to Xiao Li after knocking him over.
- Xiao Ming asked Xiao Li which class he was in.
- Xiao Ming mistook Xiao Li for a student.
- Xiao Li was happy because of what Xiao Ming said.
- Xiao Li was happy because he felt he looked young.
- Xiao Li was not angry about being knocked over or provoked.

## dnk_052efe580300a8ba — The Raging Fire

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.95  
Теги: Original_Data  

**Условие:** The fire raged. He was a hero; he was a running dog.

**Разгадка:** The hero and the running dog are the same person. As a hero, he was an undercover agent who made significant contributions by gathering intelligence from the enemy, with his deeds recorded only within his organization. As a running dog, to gather intelligence and protect his organization, he had to make many choices against his conscience, even eliminating former comrades, teachers, and innocent people. But later, he was betrayed. The traitor burned his identity documents and work records in front of him. Even if he survived, there would be no documents to prove his past and future sacrifices, and no one could step forward to vouch for his innocence.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The 'hero' and the 'running dog' are the same person.
- His identity is an undercover agent or a spy.
- The 'raging fire' destroyed important documents.
- His true identity can no longer be proven.
- The story involves betrayal and sacrifice.
- He lost the chance to prove his innocence.

## dnk_0642c50980a572d5 — Piety

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.95  
Теги: Original_Data  

**Условие:** The Creator God was very angry. With the efforts of the divine envoys, the God smiled many years later.

**Разгадка:** The Creator God created the world. When He discovered that the created humans had greatly polluted the beautiful world, and that human hearts were no longer as pure and beautiful as when they were first created, the Creator God became very angry. He found His believing divine envoys, explained all of this to them, and warned them to make changes, otherwise the power He left behind would destroy this world. The divine envoys initially spread goodwill, advocated environmental protection, and led by example, but they found it was useless. Human inherent weaknesses persisted, and the world could never become beautiful. So the divine envoys ultimately used divine power to destroy the existing civilization. Many years later, the Earth, without human civilization, regained its former vitality and beauty, and forest apes, which had not evolved into humans, regained their 'purity' in biological thought. The God saw this scene, was very satisfied, and smiled.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The Creator God is angry about human pollution of the world and moral degradation
- The divine envoys initially tried to change humanity through education
- The divine envoys found that humanity's 'inherent weaknesses' could not be changed
- The divine envoys ultimately chose to destroy existing civilization to 'purify' the world
- God's smile stems from the Earth regaining its original vitality and the 'purity' of its creatures, not from human change

**Разгадка:** I am a college student. At night, a woman in red often comes to sell door-to-door late at night, knocking on each room every night. If someone opens the door, she asks, 'Do you want red clothes?'. In the previous nights, I was very angry after being disturbed and shouted 'No'. One night, the woman came again. I finally couldn't bear it and yelled at her, 'How many red clothes do you have? I'll take them all. Stop bothering me!' I only heard the woman chuckle, turned around, and left without giving me red clothes. That night, everyone slept well, and no one came to knock on the door again. The next day, no one got up. When the dorm supervisor checked the dormitory and lifted the quilt, it was found that the skin on the upper body of me and my roommates had been peeled off, looking like wearing a red dress.

**Ключевые факты:**

- Red-clothed woman knocks on the door to sell at night
- Red clothes have a terrifying meaning
- The protagonist angrily accepts the invitation
- An angry word招致 (causes) a terrifying disaster
- Roommates are all skinned and made into red clothes

## dnk_082e2a6f4f776cf3 — Son

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.95  
Теги: Supernatural_Fantasy  

**Условие:** The son committed suicide and left a note. The mother went crazy after reading the note.

**Разгадка:** After marrying a wealthy businessman, the woman killed the wealthy businessman's original son in an accident for property. Later, she gave birth to her own son, but the son committed suicide after learning that the woman was pregnant again. The note said: You killed me, so I will make you give birth to me repeatedly and lose me again.

**Ключевые факты:**

In a daze, I tore through time and space, traveling to the past to commit evil. Suddenly, a sharp cry awakened me. My consciousness abruptly cleared, and I saw my younger self, sobbing uncontrollably. I cried, realizing that years later, my monstrous self had destroyed my own family, planting the seed of obsession in my younger self. In the future, my younger self would also transform into a monster... This was an inevitable outcome.

**Ключевые факты:**

- My family was destroyed by a monster, leading me to seek revenge
- I transformed into a monster in the future due to excessive obsession
- My monstrous self traveled through time to the past and destroyed my younger self's family
- The monster cried because it realized it was the root cause of my tragedy and transformation into a monster
- The inevitable outcome refers to an unbreakable cycle of fate, where hatred leads to one's own downfall and the repetition of tragedy

- The well is a key location; it contains not only watermelons but also a corpse.

- Xiao Qiang and Xiao Mei are the murderers of 'me' (the narrator).

Solving the instance's puzzle allows one to survive in reality. The more people killed, the more one survives in reality, yet the more people killed, the more one dies.

**Разгадка:** In the instance, only one person dies per day; once someone dies, everyone else is safe. Participants can use this rule to cause others to die before them, thereby gaining more time to solve puzzles and increasing their chances of clearing the instance and surviving in reality. However, those who die in the instance will turn into ghosts within the instance. Therefore, while killing others in this instance makes it easier to clear, in subsequent instances, the ghosts of those killed will return for revenge. The instance is already full of dangerous ghosts, and with the addition of those who were killed, this person will have virtually no chance of survival. Thus, "the more people killed, the more one can safely return to the human world, yet the more people killed, the more one dies."

**Ключевые факты:**

- Only one person is allowed to die per day in the instance, allowing others temporary safety
- Killing other participants in the instance buys oneself more time to solve puzzles
- Those who die in the instance transform into ghosts within the instance
- Individuals who clear the instance by killing others will face the ghosts of those victims in subsequent instances
- Killing more people, while beneficial for short-term survival, ultimately increases the risk of death in the long run

That night, my grandfather informed my mother of my disappearance. With the help of the police, my mother saw my body.

**Ключевые факты:**

- Made a flower wreath and prepared fruits for mother
- Walked to town to surprise mother
- Fell and hit head while picking fruit
- Bled to death in the wilderness without being noticed
- Mother saw my body in the end

**Разгадка:** The man can see people's date of death! The old woman will die when she turns 69! This means that in 5 minutes, the train will crash, and everyone on board will die.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The man has the ability to foresee the date of death.
- The 'age' he sees is actually the age of death.
- The old woman will die in five minutes.
- The old woman's death is not from natural causes.
- The train is about to have a fatal accident.
- Everyone on the train will die in five minutes.
- The man's face turned pale because he foresaw his own death.

**Разгадка:** War raged. To move the still-living baby to a safe zone, one of my hands was blown off, a bloody mess. I didn't want to scare him, so I hid my hand behind my back. Seeing me like this, he seemed to think I would suddenly pull out candy or a toy for him, just like his parents would, and he actually grinned amidst the ruins.
I could imagine his laughter; it must be more beautiful than singing, definitely crisp, clean, and refreshing. Unfortunately, I couldn't hear it. Explosions were still going off in the distance; my ears had long gone deaf from the gunfire.
'I'm sorry... little baby, Auntie might not be able to pull out a little gift for you...'
I died.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The narrator's hidden hand suffered severe physical trauma.
- The story is set against a backdrop of violence and danger (e.g., war).
- 'He' who smiled at the narrator is a young child or baby.
- The narrator's hearing loss was caused by external environmental factors.
- The narrator's apology is related to being unable to fulfill a child's expectation (e.g., producing a gift).

**Условие:** We are lost souls in hell, surviving solely on energy. Everyone hopes to return to the mortal world. I pushed with all my might and finally squeezed inside, only to realize I was terribly wrong...

**Разгадка:** Hell as a whole is shaped like a vertical jellyfish, with different strata (simulating the eighteen layers of hell). The closer one gets to the 'jellyfish's' head, the better the living environment. We all hoped to enter the 'jellyfish's' head, believing it was the gate to the human world. There are two ways to ascend a stratum: one is for people in the same stratum to see the number on the back of each other's necks (one cannot see their own through any means); in this case, both parties consume very little energy, but everyone can enter the next stratum. The other way is to kill someone in the same stratum; the killer can then ascend and gain the energy of the deceased, while the deceased can only descend. Killing here doesn't cause true death; the deceased loses the energy they need to survive and will find it harder to survive in the harsh environment. In hell, it's difficult to turn your back to someone to let them see the number on your neck, as you don't know if they will kill you the next second. So I kept killing, finally earning the right to enter the 'jellyfish's' head. We all forgot one thing: the 'jellyfish's' head is still a 'jellyfish,' so even if the environment at the top of hell is good, it is still hell. Moving upwards only leads to eternal damnation in the Avīci Hell, while moving downwards is the only way to return to the human world.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The structure of hell is jellyfish-shaped; moving upwards means entering deeper, harsher environments
- There are two ways to gain promotion, one of which is killing
- Killing does not cause true death, but it leads to the killed losing energy and falling downwards
- I chose to kill to gain promotion
- The 'Sukhavati' gate does not lead to the human world, but to a deeper cycle of hell

- The cycle of karma and guilt
- Inability to change fate
- The psychology of self-blame and atonement
- The pain and irremediable regret
- Coincidences and tragedies in life

Originally, the person with her could have saved her, but he grabbed her prosthetic limb, so the prosthesis quickly detached from her body, and Mother fell. If I hadn't given Mother the prosthetic limb, the person with her would have grabbed her other hand. So I feel like I caused Mother's death.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The phrase 'raised me single-handedly' has a literal meaning in addition to its figurative one.
- The mother had a physical disability (lost a hand).
- The narrator once provided the mother with an item to compensate for her physical defect (a prosthetic limb).
- The mother died in an accidental fall.
- The item provided by the narrator, at the time of the accident, actually hindered effective rescue.

## dnk_c43f2bb499fe50f4 — The Killer

Язык: en

Теги: Original_Data  

**Условие:** The lights dimmed, fog rolled in. The lights came on, someone was dead, but we, wearing collars that couldn't be removed, never found the killer.

**Разгадка:** Many people were confined in a building. Each time the lights dimmed, one person would remain awake, and the sprayed mist would cause others to fall unconscious. Simultaneously, each time the lights dimmed, the awake person had to kill someone, otherwise they would die from poison (the collar contained poison, which would be injected into the wearer's neck if the collar was forcibly removed or remotely controlled). Each time the lights dimmed, an image would be played—this image was the awake person's most desperate and secret memory, something they least wanted others to know. Simultaneously, the image would induce suicide in the viewer. Ultimately, all those who watched the image committed suicide, so the living never found a 'killer' or someone who died from poison.

**Ключевые факты:**

- A was commanding a real war.
- The examiner told him the truth.
- A's breakdown came from immense guilt.
- He annihilated a civilization.

- Fifth Rabbit did not die but successfully escaped.

- He ultimately chose death to avoid a worse fate at the hands of his enemies.

Сам турист в этом, как правило, не разбирается, поэтому у него спрашивают, какого цвета была змея, и по цвету определяют разновидность. **Ключевые факты:**

- Man was bitten by a snake in Thailand.
- Identifying snake species is crucial for the right antidote.
- Man was colorblind.
- Colorblindness led to wrong antidote.

Чтобы уменьшить их число, городские власти сделали обязательным пользование ремнями безопасности. Водители и пассажиры стали пристегивать эти ремни, но число ДТП осталось неизменным, а число пострадавших в них людей, которые поступали в больницу, даже увеличилось. Почему?

**Разгадка:** Пользование ремнями безопасности уменьшило число погибающих при ДТП. Многие люди, которые без ремня безопасности погибли бы (и попали бы в морги), оставались в живых, но получали травмы, и им требовалось лечение. Поэтому число попадающих в больницу стало больше.

**Ключевые факты:**

- Seat belts were made mandatory.
- The number of fatal accidents decreased.
- More people survived but were injured.
- The increased number of injured people visited the hospital.

**Разгадка:** Больной носил аппарат на здоровом ухе.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The man wore the hearing aid on the wrong ear.
- The doctor was angry because the patient made a mistake for 20 years.

- Old people misunderstood the cadets' actions as a sign of impending war.

## dnk_71d6ec5fd222866c — A funny vagrant

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.93  
Сложность: 6/10  
Теги: medium, curated, key-clues  

**Условие:** The doorbell rings. Bill opens the door. On the threshold, he sees a local vagrant. - Hello, - says the vagrant, - as usual, I was going around the garbage pits and in one of them found a wallet with $1,000 and your ID. You must have thrown it away by mistake. - Right! – says Bill joyfully. - My wallet! Thank you so much! - Please check the contents - the vagrant asks. - One thousand even! – confirms Bill, counting the bills hastily. Then he takes a $20 bill out of the pack and gives it to the vagrant. - This is from me with thanks! They part, being quite content with each other. - Who was it? – Bill’s wife asks. Bill laughs and tells his wife what happened. Why’s it funny?

**Разгадка:** When returning the wallet, the vagrant had high hopes for gratitude. But there was a chance that Bill wouldn’t have any broken money at hand. In the wallet, there were only $100 bills. Would Bill agree to pay such a large amount? And the vagrant made a wise decision. Before returning the wallet, he had exchanged one hundred for smaller bills – 5, 10, 20, 50, deciding that thus Bill would be able to choose the amount to thank him with. It was the vagrant’s forethought that made Bill laugh.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The vagrant found Bill's wallet with only $100 bills.
- The vagrant exchanged one $100 bill for smaller bills before returning the wallet.
- Bill laughed because of the vagrant's thoughtful action to provide change for a smaller reward.

**Условие:** A man in uniform stands on the beach of a tropical island. He takes out a cigarette, lights it, and begins smoking. He takes out a letter and begins reading it. The cigarette burns down between his fingers, but he doesn't throw it away. He cries. Why?

**Разгадка:** He is a guard/attendant in a leper colony. The letter (to him) tells him that he has contracted the disease. The key is the cigarette burning down between his fingers -- leprosy is fairly unique in killing off sensory nerves without destroying motor ability.

- The man is a guard/attendant in a leper colony.
- He receives a letter informing him he has contracted the disease.
- Leprosy causes loss of sensory nerves, explaining why he doesn't feel the burning cigarette.

**Условие:** If he'd turned on the light, he'd have lived. Why?

**Разгадка:** A man was shot during a robbery in his store one night. He staggered into the back room, where the telephone was, and called home, dialing by feel since he hadn't turned on the light. - He accidentally dialed a stranger instead of his family.

## dnk_2bc1d3a250f2920c — Untitled #1141

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.92  
Теги: curated, key-clues  

**Условие:** A newspaper reported that Jacques Dubois finished first in a race held in France. His average speed was given, correctly, as 19,475 km/hour. Why?

**Разгадка:** In European numbers, the comma is used the same way Americans use a decimal point. The man thus (Americans would say) ran 19.475 km/hour, which is a pretty good speed at which to run a standard-length (42.195 km) marathon. I assume most Europeans seeing this item would ask "So where's the puzzle?", but it might be a good puzzle for Americans.

**Ключевые факты:**

- European numbers use commas as decimal points
- Jacques Dubois is a marathon runner
- The race took place in France, where the European number system is used

## dnk_331390263ec5b875 — Untitled #1099

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.92  
Теги: curated, key-clues  

**Условие:** A U.S. Navy sailor on the deck of a cruiser noticed an explosive mine in the water directly in the path of the ship. With no time to communicate the situation to the captain of the ship, the sailor saved the lives of the crew and the ship. Why?

**Разгадка:** The sailor grabbed the fire hose from the deck and used the force of the water from the hose to push the mine away from the hull of the ship. The water pressure doesn't explode the mine; WWII-style mines contain magnetic sensors which make them explode on contact with a ship's hull.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The sailor noticed the mine directly in the ship's path
- There was no time to communicate with the captain
- The sailor used a fire hose to push the mine away
- WWII-style mines explode on contact with a ship's hull

## dnk_4710867bbbb7e4d7 — Untitled #1131

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.92  
Теги: curated, key-clues  

**Условие:** A man is killed on a train. He is found to have written "elf" on the floor in his own blood. Why?

**Разгадка:** Attached to the train was a caboose with a safe carrying a shipment of jewels. The victim, Schmidt, was the conductor guarding the shipment; he had robbed the safe himself, and had an accomplice traveling on the train under a false name to remove the loot. The accomplice killed Schmidt to keep his share. Schmidt didn't know the accomplice's false name, so he wrote the killer's berth number, 11. For greater clarity he spelled out the number as a word -- in his native German. (In the original story he didn't want "11" to be misread as two parallel lines, but Germans don't write "1" as a straight line.) This arguably belongs in section 2 for double meaning, but the double-meaninged word here is explicitly called out, so I'm going to leave it in section 1 for now.

**Ключевые факты:**

- Schmidt was guarding a shipment of jewels.
- The victim robbed the safe with an accomplice.
- Accomplice had a false name and was on the train.
- Schmidt wrote "elf" (11 in German) indicating the killer's berth number.
- He wrote it in German to avoid confusion with parallel lines.

## dnk_50b9bd82f1bc02d7 — Untitled #1180

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.92  
Теги: curated, key-clues  

**Условие:** A rope breaks. A bell rings. A man dies. Why?

**Разгадка:** A blind man enjoys walking near a cliff and uses the sound of a buoy to gauge his distance from the edge. One day the buoy's anchor rope breaks, allowing the buoy to drift away from the shore. When it rings, the man thinks he's further away from the edge than he is, walks over it, and falls to his death.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The man is blind.
- He relies on the buoy sound to gauge distance from the cliff edge.
- The buoy's anchor rope broke, causing it to drift away.
- The misleading sound caused him to walk over the edge.

## dnk_5d78b36536df8798 — Untitled #1102

Качество: 0.92  
Теги: curated, key-clues  

**Условие:** A man was walking down a road when a stone lodged itself between his foot and his sandal. He leaned against a pole and, with his head down to watch, he shook his foot to dislodge the stone. Another man came up and broke the first man's arm in three places. Why?

**Разгадка:** The chap shaking his foot to dislodge the stone was leanig against a metal light pole. The other fellow came along and thought that the pole had become 'live' somehow; he thought the first fellow was being electrocuted (and that the muscles in his hand had contracted and he couldn't let go). So the second fellow rushed over and whacked the first one on the arm, hard. He apologised for it afterwards.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The first man leaned against a metal light pole.
- The second man thought the first man was being electrocuted.
- The second man tried to save the first man by hitting his arm.
- The intention was to help, not to harm.

**Условие:** Two men are found dead outside of an igloo. Why?

**Разгадка:** The men have gone spelunking and have taken an Igloo cooler with them so they can have a picnic down in the caves. They cleverly used dry ice to keep their beer cold, not realizing that as the dry ice sublimed (went from a solid state to a vapor state) it would push the lighter oxygen out of the cave, and they would suffocate.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The men went spelunking.
- They brought an Igloo cooler with dry ice.
- Dry ice sublimed and displaced oxygen.
- They suffocated due to lack of oxygen.

- Contraband is hidden in an air conditioning duct

**Условие:** As I drive to work on my motorcycle, there is one corner which I go around at a certain speed whether it's rainy or sunny. If it's cloudy but not raining, however, I usually go faster. Why?

**Разгадка:** There's a car wash on that corner. On rainy days, the rain reduces traction. On sunny days, water from the car wash has the same effect. If rain is threatening, though, the car wash gets little business and thus doesn't make the road wet, so I can take the corner faster.

**Ключевые факты:**

- There's a car wash on the corner.
- Rain and car wash water reduce traction.
- On cloudy, non-rainy days, the car wash receives less business.
- Less business at the car wash means a drier and less slippery road.

**Условие:** 一名女子突然大喊着火啦!然而周围并没有发生任何火灾。(女子精神没问题)。为什么?

**Разгадка:** 因为女子当时自己在家被快递员威胁了。如果喊救命,可能作用不大。大喊着火了,大家都会出来逃命。

## dnk_cae875a374e6a1a5 — Untitled #1091

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.92  
Теги: curated, key-clues  

**Условие:** A man enters the elevator of a high rise apartment building, takes off one glove, and pushes the button for the tenth floor. The next day, the same man enters the elevator, puts on one glove, and pushes the button for the tenth floor. Why?

**Разгадка:** The man is blind. His first time in the elevator, he's wearing gloves; the elevator uses buttons that work by electrical conduction through the skin; they light up at the slightest touch, but not through a glove. The man thus has to remove a glove to get the button to work. But he discovers that first day that as he runs his ungloved hand over the buttons to find the tenth floor, all the buttons are activated, and the elevator stops at all the floors. So from then on, he carries a glove with him; he puts it on when he enters the elevator, finds the right button with his gloved hand, then uses his ungloved hand to press the tenth-floor button.

**Ключевые факты:**

- The man is blind.
- Elevator buttons work by electrical conduction through the skin.
- Braille labels on buttons not effective in preventing accidental activation.
- He uses one glove to avoid activating multiple floors.

## dnk_e917a0bd447c3394 — Untitled #1128

Язык: en  
Качество: 0.92  
Теги: curated, key-clues  

**Условие:** Two brothers are involved in a murder. Though it's clear that one of them actually committed the crime, neither can be punished. Why?

**Разгадка:** One of the brothers (A) confesses to the murder. At his trial, his brother (B) is called as the only defense witness; B immediately confesses, in graphic detail, to having committed the crime. The defense lawyer refuses to have the trial stopped, and A is acquitted under the "reasonable doubt" clause. Immediately afterward, B goes on trial for the murder; A is called as the only defense witness and he confesses. B is declared innocent; and though everyone knows that one of them did it, how can they tell who? Further, neither can be convicted of perjury until it's decided which of them did it... I don't know if that would actually work under the US legal system, but someone else who heard the story said that his father was on the jury for a very similar case in New York some years ago. Mark Brader points out that the brothers might be convicted of conspiracy to commit perjury or to obstruct justice, or something of that kind.

**Ключевые факты:**

- Both brothers confess to the crime
- Each brother is the only defense witness in the other's trial
- Acquitted under "reasonable doubt" clause
- Possible charges of conspiracy to commit perjury or obstruct justice

**Разгадка:** Mr. Box and Mr. Door had been in the navy together years ago. They had both been on a ship that had shipwrecked in the Pacific. Mr. Door had sent Mr. Box an arm in the mail. Mr. Box assumed it was Mr. Doors arm, but when Mr. Box visited Mr. Door and saw that he still had both of his arms, he became very angry that Mr. Door had not followed through on his side of the bargain and shot him.

- They survived a shipwreck together
- Mr. Door, a navy doctor, suggested amputating each survivor's left arm for food
- Mr. Door promised to amputate his arm later, but he didn't
- Mr. Box received an arm in the mail, assuming it was Mr. Door's
- Mr. Box realized Mr. Door didn't keep his promise when he saw both his arms intact

**Разгадка:** “爸爸”并不是我真正的爸爸,而是将我拐走的人贩子,而那个疯癫的女人就是一直在寻找我的妈妈,那天我跟着“爸爸”在街上行乞,她一眼就认出了被折磨的不成人形的我,人贩子见事情败露,急忙将我抱回了家,妈妈为了复仇,用人贩子折磨我的方式折磨人贩子,随后杀了他,我终于可以回家了。

**Ключевые факты:**

- 识破'工作'是乞讨
- 识破'爸爸'是人贩子
- 确认女人是生母
- 揭示'折磨'手法与复仇

## dnk_2ae3a3717164cb7b — 治病

Язык: zh  
Качество: 0.9  
Теги: logic-profile, human-reviewed-failure  

**Условие:** 他决定给经济拮据的母亲治病,却被母亲强硬地拒绝了。

**Разгадка:** 生意破产的母亲患了肾衰竭,需要肾移植,他决定将自己的肾捐给母亲。他不知道的是,自己的一个肾,早在小的时候,就被因为做生意而缺钱的母亲卖掉了。

**Ключевые факты:**

- 母亲得了肾衰竭
- 儿子试图捐肾
- 儿子少了一个肾
- 少掉的肾是儿时被母亲卖掉的

## dnk_32a7dde7714578e4 — 自相残杀

Язык: zh  
Качество: 0.9  
Теги: logic-profile, human-reviewed-failure  

**Условие:** 两兄弟在酒吧喝酒。他们开始争吵。其中一人掏枪射杀了另一人。不久后他自己也不幸身亡。

**Разгадка:** 两兄弟是连体人。其中一人抱怨另一人不讲卫生,口臭难忍,并掏枪杀死了他。他自己也因失血过多而死。

**Ключевые факты:**

- 发现两人身体有异样(衣服/距离)
- 确认死因是失血过多而非枪击(对凶手而言)
- 得知争吵原因是口臭/卫生
- 揭露连体人身份

## dnk_3d503f6d6fadae31 — 要水拿枪

Язык: zh  
Качество: 0.9  
Теги: logic-profile, human-reviewed-failure  

**Условие:** 一个男人走进一家酒吧,并向酒保要了一杯水。酒保拿出一支枪并瞄准他,该名男子说:“谢谢你!”然后离开,请问发生了什么事?

**Разгадка:** 该名男子打嗝,他希望喝一杯水来改善状况。酒保意识到这一点,选择拿枪吓他,男子一紧张之下,打嗝自然消失,因而衷心感谢酒保后就离开了。

**Ключевые факты:**

- 发现男子有生理困扰(打嗝)
- 理解要是为了治病而非解渴
- 酒保的拔枪是善意的
- 惊吓治愈了困扰

## dnk_3fe268aeba24f924 — 祭日

Язык: zh  
Качество: 0.9  
Теги: logic-profile, human-reviewed-failure  

**Условие:** 在儿子去世一周年的祭日上, 我杀死了三个来悼念他的人。

**Разгадка:** 儿子生病去世,他在临终前告诉我,把他的器官捐献给有需要的人,这样他就能以另外的方式继续活在世界上。我同意了。最后儿子身上有三个器官分别捐献给了三个不同的人。在儿子的祭日上,我认出了他们,接受皮肤捐赠的男人,居然满身都是纹身,接受肺部捐赠的小伙,不停地在那吸烟,而接受肝捐赠的居然打电话约朋友晚上出去喝酒。我儿子把生的机会留给他们,但他们竟然这样继续糟践自己。我深深为儿子感到不甘,愤怒不已的我杀了他们三个。

**Ключевые факты:**

- 儿子死于生病
- 儿子捐献了器官
- 那三人是器官受赠者
- 三人有纹身/吸烟/酗酒行为
- 我认为他们在糟践儿子的生命

Теги: logic-profile, human-reviewed-failure  

**Условие:** 我在床上躺着看直播,刷到了一个漆黑的直播间,直播间里越来越亮,我看到了天花板,然后我死了。

**Разгадка:** 我观看的这个直播间正在直播杀人,巧的是这一次要杀的人就是我。我关着灯躺在床上看直播,所以直播间里漆黑一片。主播进来后打开了灯,直播间逐渐变亮,而我也能看见天花板了。看清我位置的主播把我给杀了。

**Ключевые факты:**

- 确认直播内容是杀人直播
- 确认'漆黑'是因为我关了灯
- 确认'变亮'是因为凶手开了灯
- 确认直播画面就是我的房间
- 还原凶手看直播定位杀人的过程

## dnk_6fa3b2e035626d71 — 接连死去的哥哥

Язык: zh  
Качество: 0.9  
Теги: logic-profile, human-reviewed-failure  

**Условие:** 我有两个哥哥,我们三兄弟自小就睡在一张床上。后来有一天二哥因为生病死了,不久后我把大哥也杀了。

**Разгадка:** 我的两个哥哥是双胞胎。从小我们关系就特别好,同睡一张床。大哥睡我左边,二哥睡我右边,十几年了,我已经习惯了这样。可是有一天二哥却因为得了大病死了。我床的右边就这样空了。我很不习惯,突然我想到了!把大哥砍成两半不就好了吗,今天晚上我又睡得好香。

**Ключевые факты:**

- 知道三人的睡眠位置关系(左/中/右)
- 知道二哥死后主角产生了空虚/不平衡感
- 知道杀大哥是为了'某种功能性用途'
- 知道'砍成两半'是为了同时填补左右两边

## dnk_750374da67fc30ad — 挑衅

Язык: zh  
Качество: 0.9  
Теги: logic-profile, human-reviewed-failure  

**Условие:** 一天,游手好闲的阿星在大街上游荡。正巧碰上一所小学放学,他在拥挤的人流中不幸被无良小学生倒,小学生不仅没有道歉而且还出言挑衅阿星,阿星却没有因此生气反而很高兴,这是为什么?

**Разгадка:** 小学生很生气的说了一句:“你是哪个班的?下次带我哥揍你。”年近30的阿星没想到自己在小学生眼里看上去这么年轻,心里舒坦了很多。

**Ключевые факты:**

- 确认阿星是成年人
- 得知小学生说了什么(问班级/找哥哥)
- 理解阿星被误认为是学生
- 推出阿星因'显年轻'而高兴

## dnk_821cafc35f2b89f4 — 猛鬼说明书

Язык: zh  
Качество: 0.9  
Теги: logic-profile, human-reviewed-failure  

**Условие:** 一篇获得了短篇推理小说大赛第一名的作品原文:

以下内容专为有能力捕食人类的猛鬼提供
对人类、不具备捕食能力的鬼怪
以及其他存在毫无作用,无需阅读

1. 想办法选择那些具有强烈人类特质的猎物

2. 属于灵界的信息可以起到定位猎物的作用

3. 来自人界的信号极其不稳定
若想要成功打开通往人界的传送门
则需想办法使信号维持得更久

4. 
(字迹被某种油脂污染无法辨认)

5. 坦受那些从明的猎物 主动体出的要求

虽然费解,但我仍然开始认真阅读
希望找到它优胜的理由。

**Разгадка:** 这篇所谓的“获奖小说”其实是一本由作者和鬼怪合谋创作的诅咒说明书。
作者通过让小说获奖并广泛传播,吸引大量读者阅读。
当人们阅读这本“来自灵界的信息”时,他们的精神力会汇聚成强大的“来自人界的信号”。
这个信号足以打开“通往人界的传送门”,从而让鬼怪能够定位并捕食这些读者。
故事中的“我”正在阅读这篇小说,他/她本人就是即将被捕食的猎物。
第四条规则被油脂(暗示是之前受害者的脂肪)涂抹,很可能隐藏了自救的关键信息。

**Ключевые факты:**

- 发现目标读者是鬼怪
- 理解阅读行为即为发射信号
- 识破作者的共谋身份
- 确认油脂是人油且自己是猎物

## dnk_946c31ea302de438 — 姐妹难分

Язык: zh  
Качество: 0.9  
Теги: logic-profile, human-reviewed-failure  

**Условие:** 一个雨天,男人拉着一个大行李箱出门。他在门口碰见了自己的妻子,和妻子兴奋地说了几句话后,他神色忽然古怪至极。他仔细看了看妻子的侧脸,看了看手表,又转头看了看门外的大雨。而后他慌慌张张拉着行李箱走了,从此销声匿迹。

**Разгадка:** 女人有个长相一模一样的双胞胎姐姐。女人老公偷偷出轨双胞胎姐姐。双胞胎姐姐与女人老公偷情时,为了把自己和女人区别开来,会在侧脸画一颗显眼的痣。最近,女人的老公已经完全厌倦女人,一直在找机会杀了女人。一个雨天,女人照常出门工作。趁此机会,老公又邀请了姐姐来家里偷情。老公发现坐在沙发上的这个女人脸上没有痣,他十分慌乱,以为妻子突然回家。担心偷情败露,他打算今天就杀死妻子。于是他悄悄走过去杀死女人,装进行李箱。出门后,他在门外遇见一个女人,起初他以为是姐姐——自己的情人,于是兴奋地说了几句话。说话后,他发现不对。仔细一看,这个女的脸上也没有痣。他看手表,发现是妻子往常下班回家的时间。今天一直在下大雨。他突然明白,刚才家里的那个女人就是姐姐。不过因为是雨天,她脸上的痣被雨水洗掉了。他杀错了人。震惊后怕之余,他逃走了。

**Ключевые факты:**

- 存在长得一模一样的两个人(双胞胎)
- 死者是情妇(姐姐)
- 区分两人的标记是痣(画上去的)
- 雨水洗掉了标记导致误杀
- 出门看表确认了杀错人

## dnk_95e95445e87d5685 — 对赌

Язык: zh  
Качество: 0.9  
Теги: logic-profile, human-reviewed-failure  

**Условие:** 两个死人,现场只有一把枪,一颗子弹,一副牌。发生了什么?

**Разгадка:** 两个人在潜艇里,潜艇在深水因故障进水,两个人赌牌,赢的人才可以用枪自杀,体面死去。输的人只能在潜艇中痛苦地死亡。

**Ключевые факты:**

- 确认两人被困在密闭空间
- 确认身处深海/潜艇
- 确认面临不可避免的死亡威胁(缺氧/水压)
- 确认赌博是为了争取自杀(解脱)的机会
- 还原完整故事

**Разгадка:** 我是一个盲人,爸爸不放心我出门每次都会悄悄跟上,可我却不知道一直以为有人尾随。有一天,一辆失控的卡车向我冲了过来,千钧一发之际爸爸从后面跑过来推开了我,自己却葬身车下。脚步声终于变成一个人的了,可是爸爸却永远离开了我。

- 意识到主角有视力障碍
- 确认另一个人是亲人(父亲)

- 理解后悔的真正含义(父亲牺牲)

## dnk_4c0c6f2b845db121 — Позови, и я приду!

Язык: ru

**Условие:** Мэри позвала Генриха. Генрих пришел, но не смог сориентироваться в ситуации... и умер!

**Разгадка:** Сюжет навеян романом "Аэропорт" Артура Хэйли. В те времена, когда аэропорты уже существовали, а переносные рации - еще нет, существовала проблема - как созвать всех охраняющих аэропорт полицейских в одно место и при этом не наводить паники среди посетителей аэропорта. Решалась она так: выбирали чрезвычайно редкую комбинацию имени и фамилии, сообщали ее перед началом дня всем полицейским и, если требовалось собрать полицейских, по громкоговорящей связи просили человека с этим именем и фамилией прибыть в необходимое место. Вероятность совпадения с реальным человеком, находящемся в аэропорту, почти нулевая. Почти... Генрих - террорист-одиночка с бомбой в чемодане, собирался сесть на самолет и взорвать его в воздухе (прообраз - Герреро из "Аэропорта"). Однако он так волновался, что умудрился потерять паспорт и обнаружил пропажу уже в здании аэропорта. Он уже совсем было собирался отложить свой план, как вдруг услышал объявление по радио, что человека с его именем и фамилией просят подойти к администратору аэропорта. Он, разумеется, пошел, будучи в полной уверенности, что нашли его паспорт. Откуда же ему было знать, что паспорта никто не находил - просто его имя и фамилия совпали с кодовыми именем и фамилией для сбора полицейских. Когда он открыл дверь в комнату администратора и обнаружил там полтора десятка блюстителей закона, он подумал, что раскрыт, и взорвал бомбу. Автор: avgera. http://www.danetka.ru/cgi-bin/info.pl?uid=1972

**Разгадка:** Человек мучился от икоты и зашел в ближайший бар выпить воды. Бармен понял, в чем его проблема, и применил испытанное средство — напугать икающего человека. Способ сработал и мужчина поблагодарил его.

**Условие:** Я работаю курьером и иногда по работе мне приходится бывать в злачных районах города. Как-то раз я доставлял посылку в старое здание в одном из неспокойных районов Токио. ## dnk_0a34e4539bb0ecdf — Фантом

Язык: ru  
Качество: 0.8643  
Сложность: 6/10  
Теги: детективные, на реальных событиях  

**Условие:** Немецкая полиция совершенно растеряна. Уже на протяжении 15-ти лет один и тот же человек совершает кражи, убийства и угоны. К 2008 году они потратили 14 тысяч рабочих часов и более 15 миллионов евро, чтобы найти преступника, но так и не нашли его. Как так получилось? Это реальная история.

**Разгадка:** Главной подозреваемой была женщина, ДНК которой было обнаружено на каждом месте преступления. Но найти её не удавалось. Предполагалось, что она ведет кочевой образ жизни, потому что преступления встречались по всей Германии, а иногда и за её пределами - во Франции и Австрии. В 2009 году полиция наконец выяснила, что это была 71-летняя полька, которая много лет работала упаковщиком ватных палочек на баварской фабрике. Именно этими палочками делали ДНК-тесты. Случай вошел в историю под названием "Фантом из Хайльбронна".

**Разгадка:** Дима знал что его жена изменяет ему, но он знал лишь имя любовника. Жена клялась ему, что никакого любовника нет. Но получив результаты анализов он увидел там имя врача, совпадавшего с именем любовника. Он понял, что жена изменяет ему с врачом и не смог справиться с этим.
